Accounting_Companies

 Column NameDataTypeDefaultRefers ToDescription
🔑Accounting_Company_IDint 
*Company_Namenvarchar(75) The legal name of your organization. This name will print when no logo is found on a statement. Attach a logo to this record to show it on your statement.
 Company_Contact_IDint⊶ ContactsThe contact record of the organization containing the organization address and phone numbers.
 Default_Congregationint⊶ CongregationsEnables the Global Filter on the Statements page. Leave this option blank except in the rare case where the Accounting Company has only a single Congregation.
*Show_Onlinebit(1) If you have multiple accounting companies and wish one or more to be hidden from users of the public portal, set this value to false/no.
 Online_Sort_Ordersmallint The order in which this accounting company should be presented in relationship to other accounting companies to an end user on the my contribution statements page of the public portal.
 General_Statement_Settingsdp_Separator:bit 
 Pledge_Campaign_IDint⊶ Pledge_CampaignsThe campaign for which a donor with a pledge should see a pledge recap including their pledge balance in the top corner of their donor statement.
 Alternate_Pledge_Campaignint⊶ Pledge_CampaignsA second, additional campaign for which a donor with a pledge should see a pledge recap including their pledge balance in the top corner of their donor statement.
*List_Non_Cash_Giftsbit(1) If true, donations will be listed on a statement even for payment types where the amount will not be deductible, like non-cash or gift-in-kind.
 Statement_Footernvarchar(500) The note that will appear on the statement. Generally this contains the "no goods or services provided" IRS disclaimer.
 Statement_Letternvarchar(max) A note from senior leadership regarding finances that may appear on a specific statement designed to print this content in-line, with the statement as a separate page.
 Standard_Statement_Settingsdp_Separator:bit 
 Statement_Cutoff_Datedatetime Donors who authenticate online will be able to see donations on their statements up through this date.
 Statement_Cutoff_Automation_IDint(1)⊶ Statement_Cutoff_AutomationSelect a value, other than manual, if you want your statement cutoff date to be updated automatically.
 Standard_Statementint⊶ dp_ReportsA report designed specifically to work with our statement routine which attaches files to Statement records. Do not change this without validating the report. Contact support@ministryplatform.com for assistance.
*Formal_Salutationbit(0) If true, the greeting that will appear above the address block of your Donor Statements will use the Donor's title (Prefix) as well as their First Name instead of Nickname.
*Archive_Day_of_Yearint(46) The day of the year when prior year Statements will be automatically archived. Must be between 46 (Feb 15) and 121 (April 30th Generally). Default is 46. Once archived, the Statement record is no longer updated nor Donors or Donations added by the routine.
*Rows_Per_Pageint(26) The number of donation rows that fit safely on a single contribution statement page. 26 rows is recommended. Values between 15 and 30 are allowed. Value higher than 26 must be carefully tested.
*Summary_Columnsint(3) The number of columns on your statement that will summarize Statement Headers. For example, if set to 4, then the first 3 Statement Headers will be explicitly listed, and Donations to Programs under those headers will be summarized in their respective columns. The final summary column "Other" will list Donations to all other Programs including a detailed description. Allowed values are from 1 to 6.
 ACH_Settingsdp_Separator:bit 
 Immediate_Destination_IDnvarchar(10) Routing Number + Check Digit for the immediate destination or ACH Operator
 Immediate_Origin_IDnvarchar(10) Nine digit Federal Tax ID or other ID given by your bank
 Immediate_Destination_Namenvarchar(23) Your bank or ACH operators name
 Immediate_Origin_Namenvarchar(23) Your bank or ACH operators name
 Immediate_Routing_Numbernvarchar(9) This is always the routing number of the immediate origin. This is usually the banks routing number. It may be the same as the immediate origin ID.
 Receiving_DFI_IDnvarchar(9) Nine-digit Routing Number for your bank
*Domain_IDint⊶ dp_Domains
 Other_Settingsdp_Separator:bit 
*Current_Settingsbit There should only be one record on the accounting company page for each separate legal entity with this value set to true. If multiple records exist for a legal entity, only one record containing the current settings should have this value set to true.

⊶CongregationsAccounting_Company_IDThe accounting company or entity within which the income and expenses of this congregation are tracked.
⊶Contribution_StatementsAccounting_Company_IDThe Accounting Company associated with this Statement.

Addresses

 Column NameDataTypeDefaultRefers ToDescription
🔑Address_IDint The physical mailing address of the individuals who live in this household.
*Address_Line_1nvarchar(75) Generally the street name and house number and unit number goes in this field.
 Address_Line_2nvarchar(75) Use this field if the length of Address_Line_1 is insufficient.
 Citynvarchar(50) The town or municipality in which this address is found.
 State/Regionnvarchar(50) For USA addresses, the two-letter designation of the State in which this address is located. For international addresses this may be used for the province or region.
 Postal_Codenvarchar(15) For USA addresses the 5 or 9 letter postal code used to route mail to this address.
 Foreign_Countrynvarchar(255) TO BE DEPRECATED IN 2025: The name in ALL CAPS of the country where this address is located. Use UNITED STATES or leave blank for USA addresses.
 Country_Codenvarchar(25) A two- or three-letter code used to represent the country in which this address is located. US or USA are used for addresses in the United States. This field can be left blank.
 Carrier_Routenvarchar(10) A code applied by the Address Validator Tool to aid in delivery of mail to this address.
 Lot_Numbernvarchar(10) A value applied, if available, by the Address Validator Tool to aid in delivery of mail to this address.
 Delivery_Point_Codenvarchar(3) A value applied, if available, by the Address Validator Tool to aid in delivery of mail to this address.
 Delivery_Point_Check_Digittinyint A value applied, if available, by the Address Validator Tool to aid in delivery of mail to this address.
 Latitudenvarchar(15) The angular distance of this address on a north or south axis as it relates to the earths equator. This field may be updated by the Map My Selection tool.
 Longitudenvarchar(15) The angular distance of this address on a east or west axis as it relates to the meridian at Greenwich, England. This field may be updated by the Map My Selection tool.
 Altitudenvarchar(15) The elevation of this address as it relates to sea level. This value may be updated by the Map My Selection Tool.
 Time_Zonenvarchar(50) The region in which this address is located that observes a uniform standard time for legal, commercial, and social purposes.
 Bar_Codenvarchar(50) The Intelligent Mail Barcode is a 65-bar barcode for use on mail in the US.
 Area_Codenvarchar(50) The dialing prefix appended to a 7-digit USA phone number. The associated value may be applied to the physical addresses by the Address Validator Tool.
 Last_Validation_Attemptdatetime The date when the Address Validator Tool last validated this address.
 Countynvarchar(50) The political and geographic subdivision of a state in which this address is located. This value is not needed for mailing labels. It may be applied by the Address Validator Tool.
 Validatedbit In indication as to whether this address has been validated or deemed valid in a previous validation attempt by the Address Validator Tool.
*Do_Not_Validatebit(0) If this value is set to TRUE, the Address Validtor Tool will ignore this address.
 Last_GeoCode_Attemptdatetime The date when this address was last checked against a geocoding service. This may be updated by the Map My Selection tool.
*Domain_IDint⊶ dp_Domains
 Countrynvarchar(100) FUTURE IN 2025: The name in ALL CAPS of the country where this address is located. Use UNITED STATES or leave blank for USA addresses.

Background_Checks

 Column NameDataTypeDefaultRefers ToDescription
🔑Background_Check_IDint 
*Contact_IDint⊶ ContactsThe contact record of the person undergoing the background check.
 Requesting_Ministryint⊶ MinistriesAn optional field designating the ministry department that requested that this person undergo a background check.
 Background_Check_Submitteddatetime The date when this background check was submitted to the service provider.
 Background_Check_Returneddatetime The date when the background check provider returned the completed background check about this contact.
 All_Clearbit A flag indicating whether this contact was cleared by this background check.
 Notesnvarchar(500) Free-form notes about this background check can be stored here.
 Theftbit Set to true if this background check indicated the individual had a prior history of theft.
 Drugsbit Set to true if this background check indicated the individual had a prior history with drugs.
 Sexualbit Set to true if this background check indicated the individual had a prior history of sexual misconduct.
 DUIbit Set to true if this background check indicated the individual had a prior history of driving under the influence.
 Batterybit Set to true if this background check indicated the individual had a prior history of physical altercations.
 Trafficbit Set to true if this background check indicated the individual had a prior history of traffic violations.
 Otherbit Set to true if this background check indicated the individual had a prior history involving other infractions not explicitly listed on the background check form.
*Domain_IDint⊶ dp_Domains

 Report_Urldp_URL:varchar(2048) Link directly to the background check report provided by your third party background check vendor.
 Background_Check_Type_IDint⊶ Background_Check_TypesThe type of background check that has been requested.

 First_Namenvarchar(50) The first name of the applicant being background checked

dp_Process_Steps

 Column NameDataTypeDefaultRefers ToDescription
🔑Process_Step_IDint 
*Step_Namenvarchar(50) A short description that will describe this step and will also appear as the title of any task associated with this step.
 Instructionsnvarchar(500) Instructions designed to assist those who are assigned a task associated with this step. These instructions will appear in the body of the task.
*Process_Step_Type_IDint⊶ dp_Process_Step_TypesWhat this task will do. Depending on the value selected here the step will either create a task, request approval, send a message, or run a procedure.
*Escalation_Onlybit(0) If this value is true, this step will be skipped and invoked only by another step that has exceeded the task deadline.
*Ordersmallint The numerical order in which this step will fire in relation to other steps in this process. In a single step process this value should be 1.
*Process_IDint⊶ dp_ProcessesThe process to which this step belongs.
 Specific_Userint⊶ dp_UsersIf this step will always be owned by a specific user, set that user here. This is the user that will get the task OR be listed as having sent this email if the step sends an email. Use a generic account for steps that run a procedure.
*Supervisor_Userbit When set to "true" the step will assign a task to the supervisor of the user who edited or added the record that caused workflow to fire.
 Lookup_User_Fieldnvarchar(1000) Dynamically look up the user to be assigned the task or be listed as sending the email based on the main record. Generally the value placed in this field will end in "User_ID" or "User_Account". The table and field lookup convention used by Advanced Search is relevant here.
*Domain_IDint⊶ dp_Domains
 Escalate_to_Stepint⊶ dp_Process_StepsIf the deadline for a task created by this step is passed, select the step to which it will escalate.
 Task_Deadlinesmallint The deadline in hours by which this task must be completed. The start of the task will be when it is created and the end date will be computed based upon this value. If left blank, the end date will be 5 days from the start date.
 Email_Templateint⊶ dp_Communication_TemplatesThe record from the Templates page that will become the body of the email in the "Send an Email" step. Valid merge fields must be present on the "All Records" view of the page to which this Process is associated.
 To_Specific_Contactint⊶ ContactsIf the same contact should always be notified by this step, select them in this field. Make sure they have an email address on their contact record.
 Email_To_Contact_Fieldnvarchar(1000) Dynamically look up the contact to be sent an email based on the main record. Generally the value in this field will end in "Contact_ID". The table and field lookup convention used by Advanced Search is relevant here. If this field is utilized, you must ensure that the Contact record this field is mapped to always has a valid e-mail address.
 SQL_Statementnvarchar(1000) A valid T-SQL statement of 1000 characters or less. It may reference the dp_RecordID parameter so changes can be applied in relationship to the record which triggered this process.
 Webhook_IDint⊶ dp_WebhooksThe webhook from the Webhooks page that will be called in the "Call Webhook" step. Ensure that the Webhook record has the same Table_Name as the Process associated with this Process Step.
 Text_Templateint⊶ dp_Communication_TemplatesThe record from the Templates page that will become the content of the text in the "Send a Text" step. Valid merge fields must be present on the "All Records" view of the page to which this Process is associated.
 Text_To_Contact_Fieldnvarchar(1000) Dynamically look up the contact to be sent a text based on the main record. Generally the value in this field will end in "Contact_ID". The table and field lookup convention used by Advanced Search is relevant here. If this field is utilized, you must ensure that the Contact record this field is mapped to always has a valid mobile phone.
 Specific_User_Group_IDint⊶ dp_User_GroupsIf this step will be shared between Users, set the User Group here.
 Completion_Rule_IDint⊶ dp_Completion_RulesIndicate which rule must be satisfied for this Process Step to complete.

dp_Processes

 Column NameDataTypeDefaultRefers ToDescription
🔑Process_IDint 
*Process_Namenvarchar(50) A short descriptive title for the workflow (Ex. "Event Approval"). Keep the name as short as possible.
*Process_Managerint⊶ dp_UsersThe MinistryPlatform user who is responsible for this Process.
*Activebit Must be set to "True" for this workflow to fire.
 Descriptionnvarchar(255) A longer explanation of the purpose of this workflow process.
*Domain_IDint⊶ dp_Domains
 On_Submitnvarchar(500) An SQL statement that will be part of the SET clause of an UPDATE statement which will run when workflow is submitted (EX. _Approved = 0).
 On_Completenvarchar(500) An SQL statement that will be part of the SET clause of an UPDATE statement which will run when the final step of the workflow completes successfully (EX. _Approved =1).
 Trigger_Fieldsnvarchar(255) A field or fields on the target record which will trigger the Process when created or updated. Separate multiple fields with commas. Use the Primary Key only if you want the Process to fire only on create, not edit. Any field in the list will trigger the Process. (Ex. Event_Start_Date, Event_End_Date, Visibility_Level_ID). Leave this blank to trigger the Process for changes to any field.
 Dependent_Conditionnvarchar(4000) An SQL statement that will be used in a WHERE clause as additional criteria to determine if the record that was edited should trigger workflow (Ex. Event_Start_Date >= GetDate())
*Trigger_On_Createbit(1) If True, this Process evaluates the trigger field and dependent condition when a new record in the defined Table Name is created.
*Trigger_On_Updatebit(1) If True, this Process evaluates the trigger field and dependent condition when an existing record in the defined Table Name is updated.
*Table_Namedp_TableName:nvarchar(75) The table to which this workflow applies. This is the table where the record is added or edited that causes the workflow to trigger.

This field must have a value (0.00 if no deposit required) for a Mission Trip to be available for Registration.
